<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>
<s> on the wall close to each cell door hangs a little square board with the prisoner's name number and record <\s>
<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>
<s> the warder instructor a bearded man in blue uniform with an apron and some dangling keys is just emerging from one of the cells <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>
<s> on the wall close to each cell door hangs a little square board with the prisoner's name number and record <\s>
<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>
<s> on the wall close to each cell door hangs a little square board with the prisoner's name number and record <\s>
<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>
<s> the warder instructor a bearded man in blue uniform with an apron and some dangling keys is just emerging from one of the cells <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>

<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>

<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>

<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>
<s> on the wall close to each cell door hangs a little square board with the prisoner's name number and record <\s>
<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>
<s> the warder instructor a bearded man in blue uniform with an apron and some dangling keys is just emerging from one of the cells <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>
<s> on the wall close to each cell door hangs a little square board with the prisoner's name number and record <\s>
<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>
<s> the warder instructor a bearded man in blue uniform with an apron and some dangling keys is just emerging from one of the cells <\s>
<s> speaking from the door into the cell i'll have another bit for you when that's finished <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>
<s> on the wall close to each cell door hangs a little square board with the prisoner's name number and record <\s>
<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>
<s> the warder instructor a bearded man in blue uniform with an apron and some dangling keys is just emerging from one of the cells <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>

<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>
<s> on the wall close to each cell door hangs a little square board with the prisoner's name number and record <\s>
<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>
<s> the warder instructor a bearded man in blue uniform with an apron and some dangling keys is just emerging from one of the cells <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>
<s> on the wall close to each cell door hangs a little square board with the prisoner's name number and record <\s>
<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>

<s> scene ii part of the ground corridor of the prison <\s>
<s> the walls are coloured with greenish distemper up to a stripe of deeper green about the height of a man's shoulder and above this line are whitewashed <\s>
<s> the floor is of blackened stones <\s>
<s> daylight is filtering through a heavily barred window at the end <\s>
<s> the doors of four cells are visible <\s>
<s> each cell door has a little round peep hole at the level of a man's eye covered by a little round disc which raised upwards affords a view o f the cell <\s>
<s> on the wall close to each cell door hangs a little square board with the prisoner's name number and record <\s>
<s> overhead can be seen the iron structures of the first floor and second floor corridors <\s>
